Provincial Assemblies: 2 second delays\n   - Law Portal: 1-2 second delays\n   - District Courts: 3-5 second delays (large database)\n\n2. **robots.txt Compliance**\n   - All sources: Check and respect robots.txt\n   - Use User-Agent string identifying your crawler\n\n3. **Error Handling**\n   - Implement exponential backoff for timeouts\n   - Handle HTTP 429 (Too Many Requests)\n   - Respect 503 (Service Unavailable)\n\n4. **Data Structure**\n   - National Assembly: Query parameters (type, status) change pagination/filtering\n   - Provincial sites: Varied parameter structures\n   - Use a base URL + parameter builder\n\n### Recommended Crawl Order\n\n1. **Phase 1 (Foundation)**: National Assembly + Senate (federal level)\n2. **Phase 2 (Provincial)**: Punjab, Sindh, KPK, Balochistan assemblies\n3. **Phase 3 (Supplementary)**: Open Parliament Pakistan, Law Portal\n4. **Phase 4 (Judicial)**: Federal Courts, District Courts (with TOS review)\n\n### Data Format Strategy\n\n- **Primary**: HTML parsing for bill listings\n- **Secondary**: PDF extraction for full text (use pdfplumber or similar)\n- **Storage**: Structured database (bill_number, title, status, full_text, source_url, scraped_date)\n\n### Known Limitations\n\n- Intermittent timeout issues (possible rate limiting or server issues)\n- No official APIs documented for most sources\n- PDF-based storage means OCR may be needed for searchability\n- District courts case database is very large (8M+ cases)\n- Some sources mix HTML and PDF content\n\n---\n\n## DATA VOLUME ESTIMATES\n\n### **Short-term**: All Provincial Assemblies\n⚠ **Caution Required**: Federal Courts, District Courts (review TOS)\n\n### Suggested Architecture\n\n```\nLegal AI Crawler\n├── Config Layer\n│   ├── Source definitions (URLs, parameters)\n│   ├── Rate limiting rules\n│   └── robots.txt policies\n├── Extraction Layer\n│   ├── HTML parser (for bill listings)\n│   ├── PDF extractor (for full text)\n│   └── Metadata extractor\n├── Storage Layer\n│   ├── PostgreSQL (structured data)\n│   └── Blob storage (PDFs)\n└── Queue Layer\n    ├── Task distribution\n    └── Error handling\n```\n\n### Critical Tasks Before Launch\n\n1. **Verify robots.txt** on each domain\n2. **Review Terms of Service** (especially for district courts)\n3. **Test timeout handling** under various network conditions\n4. **Implement All bills\n/bills.php?type=1                       # Government bills\n/bills.php?type=2                       # Private member bills\n/bills.php?status=pass                  # Passed bills\n/bills-15.php?status=pass               # From NA\n```\n\n**Parameter Reference**:\n- `catid=186` → Bills category\n- `subcatid=276` → Specific legislation\n- `type=1` → Government\n- `type=2` → Passed\n\n**Extraction Fields**:\n- Bill Number\n- Title\n- Date\n- Sponsor\n- Status\n- Committee information\n\n**Implementation Notes**:\n- Complex query structure but consistent\n- Use parameter builder to construct URLs\n- Handle category/subcategory navigation\n- Store parameter mappings for reference\n\n---\n\n#### 1.3 Punjab Law Portal (PITB)\n\n**Base URL**: `https://pitb.gov.pk/law_portal` or `https://law.punjab.gov.pk/law_portal`\n\n**Coverage**: All Punjab legislation\n\n**Features**:\n- Full-text search capability\n- Covers Bills, Acts, Rules, Notifications\n- Searchable database (HTML forms)\n\n**Implementation Notes**:\n- POST-based search (likely)\n- Very large database\n- Slow search response times possible\n- Consider direct HTML index if available\n- Rate limit aggressively (1-2 second delays)\n\n**Extraction Strategy**:\n1. Identify searchable categories\n2. Query each category systematically\n3. Extract results from search pages\n4. Follow links to full text (PDF/HTML)\n\n---\n\n### TIER 2: MEDIUM PRIORITY (Provincial)\n\n#### 2.1 Punjab Assembly\n\n**Base URL**: `https://pap.gov.pk/`\n\n**Bill Endpoints**:\n```\n/bills/show/en 1: Source Configuration\n\n```python\n# sources.py\nSOURCES = {\n    'national_assembly': {\n        'base_url': 'https://www.na.gov.pk/en/',\n        'bill_endpoints': [\n            {'path': 'bills.php', 'params': {}},\n            {'path': 'bills.php', 'params': {'type': '1'}},\n            {'path': 'bills.php', 'params': {'type': '2'}},\n            {'path': 'bills.php', 'params': {'status': 'pass'}},\n        ],\n        'rate_limit_seconds': 2,\n        'timeout_seconds': 10,\n        'verify_ssl': True,\n        'extract_fields': ['bill_number', 'title', 'date', 'type', 'status'],\n        'document_url_pattern': r'/uploads/documents/(.+?).pdf'\n    },\n    # ... more sources\n}\n```\n\n### Module 2: HTML Extraction\n\n```python\n# extractors.py\nclass extract bill records\n\n        Returns:\n            List of dicts with:\n            - bill_number: str\n            - title: str\n            - date_introduced: str (YYYY-MM-DD)\n            - pdf_path: str) -> Dict:\n        \"\"\"Extract PDF metadata\"\"\"\n        pass\n```\n\n### Module 3: Data Storage\n\n```python\n# models.py\nclass Bill(BaseModel):\n    id: UUID\n    source: str  # 'national_assembly', 'senate', etc.\n    bill_number: str\n    title: str\n    date_introduced: datetime\n    date_passed: Optional[datetime]\n    bill_type: str  # 'Government' | 'Private Member'\n    status: str  # 'Passed', 'Pending', etc.\n    mover: Optional[str]\n    committee: Optional[str]\n    summary: Optional[str]\n    full_text: str  # Extracted from PDF\n    source_url: str\n    document_url: str\n    scraped_at: datetime\n    updated_at: datetime\n\n    class Config:\n        json_schema_extra = {\n            'example': {\n                'bill_number': '91 of 2025',\n                'title': 'Some Amendment Bill, 2025',\n                'date_introduced': '2025-06-15',\n                'status': 'Passed',\n                'source': 'national_assembly'\n            }\n        }\n```\n\n### Module 4: Crawler Queue Management\n\n```python\n# queue_manager.py\nclass CrawlerQueue:\n    \"\"\"Manage crawl tasks with rate limiting\"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, source_config: Dict):\n        self.config = source_config\n        self.last_request_time = {}\n\n    def add_task(self, url: str, priority: int = 0):\n        \"\"\"Add URL to crawl queue\"\"\"\n        pass\n\n    def get_next_task(self) -> Optional[str]:\n        \"\"\"Get next URL respecting rate limits\"\"\"\n        # Check if enough time has passed since last request\n        # Return URL if ready, None if rate-limited\n        pass\n\n    def mark_complete(self, url: str, status: str):\n        \"\"\"Mark task as complete/failed\"\"\"\n        pass\n```\n\n### Module 5: Error Handling\n\n```python\n# errors.py\nclass CrawlerError(Exception):\n    \"\"\"Base crawler error\"\"\"\n    pass\n\nclass RateLimitedError(CrawlerError):\n    \"\"\"Server returned rate limit error\"\"\"\n    pass\n\nclass TimeoutError(CrawlerError):\n    \"\"\"Request timeout\"\"\"\n    pass\n\nclass PDFExtractionError(CrawlerError):\n    \"\"\"Failed to extract from PDF\"\"\"\n    pass\n\n# Retry strategies\nclass RetryStrategy:\n    @staticmethod\n    def exponential_backoff(attempt: int, base_delay: int = 2) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Return delay in seconds: 2, 4, 8, 16, 32...\"\"\"\n        return base_delay ** min(attempt, 5)\n```\n\n---\n\n## FIELD MAPPING ACROSS SOURCES\n\n### Standard Bill Fields (Normalized)\n\n```\nDatabase Schema:\n- pk_id: UUID (primary key)\n- source_identifier: str (e.g., 'na_2025_91')\n- bill_number: str (e.g., '91 of 2025')\n- legislative_body: enum ('National Assembly', 'Senate', 'Punjab Assembly', etc.)\n- province: str (null for federal, 'Punjab', 'Sindh', etc.)\n- title_en: str\n- title_ur: Optional[str] (where available)\n- bill_type: enum ('Government', 'Private Member', 'Constitutional Amendment')\n- introduction_date: date\n- introduction_sitting: Optional[str] (session/sitting reference)\n- mover_name: str\n- mover_party: Optional[str]\n- current_status: enum ('Introduced', 'Referred to Committee', 'Passed', 'Rejected', 'Pending')\n- status_date: date (last status update)\n- committee_referred: Optional[str]\n- committee_report_received: bool\n- passed_date: Optional[date]\n- votes_for: Optional[int]\n- votes_against: Optional[int]\n- votes_abstain: Optional[int]\n- assent_date: Optional[date]\n- act_number: Optional[str] (if passed)\n- related_ordinances: Optional[List[str]]\n- full_text_url: str\n- full_text_format: enum ('PDF', 'HTML', 'Both')\n- full_text_language: enum ('English', 'Urdu', 'Both')\n- extracted_text: Optional[str] (OCR'd if needed)\n- summary: Optional[str] (AI-generated)\n- key_clauses: Optional[List[str]]\n- amendments: Optional[List[Dict]] (bill amendments)\n- related_bills: Optional[List[str]] (cross-references)\n- source_url: str (where crawled from)\n- crawled_at: datetime\n- last_updated: datetime\n- data_quality_score: float (0-1)\n```\n\n---\n\n## EXTRACTION PATTERNS\n\n### Pattern 1: National Assembly Bills Table\n\n```html\n<table>\n<tr>\n  <td>91 of 2025</td>\n  <td><a href=\"/bills-details.php?id=123\">Bill Title Here</a></td>\n  <td>2025-06-15</td>\n  <td>Government</td>\n  <td>Passed</td>\n  <td><a href=\"/uploads/documents/abc123.pdf\">PDF</a></td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n```\n\n**XPath/CSS Selectors**:\n```\nBill Number: td[0]\nTitle & Link: td[1] > a\nDate: td[2]\nType: td[3]\nStatus: td[4]\nDocument: td[5] > a::attr(href)\n```\n\n---\n\n### Pattern 2: Provincial Assembly Listings\n\n```html\n<div class=\"bill-item\">\n  <h3>Bill Title</h3>\n  <span class=\"bill-number\">123 of 2025</span>\n  <span class=\"date\">2025-01-15</span>\n  <span class=\"status\">Passed</span>\n  <a href=\"/bills/123\" class=\"details\">Details</a>\n</div>\n```\n\n**CSS Selectors**:\n```\n.bill-item\n  h3 → title\n  .bill-number → number\n  .date → date\n  .status → status\n  a.details::attr(href) → details_url\n```\n\n---\n\n## PDF EXTRACTION STRATEGY\n\n### For Bill Full Text\n\n```python\nimport pdfplumber\n\ndef extract_bill_text(pdf_path: str) -> Dict:\n    \"\"\"Extract text and metadata from bill PDF\"\"\"\n    with pdfplumber.open(pdf_path) as pdf:\n        metadata = pdf.metadata\n\n        # Extract all text\n        full_text = '\\n'.join(page.extract_text() for page in pdf.pages)\n\n        # Detect sections (typical bill structure)\n        sections = detect_sections(full_text)\n\n        return {\n            'full_text': full_text,\n            'page_count': len(pdf.pages),\n            'creation_date': metadata.get('CreationDate'),\n            'title': metadata.get('Title'),\n            'sections': sections,\n            'tables': extract_tables(pdf)\n        }\n```\n\n### Bill Structure Recognition\n\n```python\n# Typical Pakistan bill structure\nBILL_SECTIONS = [\n    r'^A BILL$',\n    r'^OBJECTS AND REASONS$',\n    r'^STATEMENT OF OBJECTS AND REASONS',\n    r'^\\d+\\.\\s+Short title and commencement',\n    r'^\\d+\\.\\s+Definitions',\n    r'^\\d+\\.\\s+[A-Z]',  # Section headings\n    r'^SCHEDULE$',\n]\n\ndef detect_bill_sections(text: str) -> Dict[str, Tuple[int, int]]:\n    \"\"\"Identify section boundaries in bill text\"\"\"\n    pass\n```\n\n---\n\n## RATE LIMITING CONFIGURATION\n\n### Per-Source Rate Limits\n\n```python\nRATE_LIMITS = {\n    'national_assembly': {\n        'requests_per_second': 0.5,        # 2 second delay\n        'concurrent_connections': 1,\n        'timeout_seconds': 10,\n        'retry_on_timeout': True,\n        'max_retries': 3,\n        'backoff_factor': 2\n    },\n    'senate': {\n        'requests_per_second': 0.5,\n        'concurrent_connections': 1,\n        'timeout_seconds': 10,\n    },\n    'punjab_law_portal': {\n        'requests_per_second': 1.0,         # 1 second delay (safer for large DB)\n        'concurrent_connections': 1,\n        'timeout_seconds': 15,\n    },\n    'district_courts': {\n        'requests_per_second': 0.2,         # 5 second delay (VERY large DB)\n        'concurrent_connections': 1,\n        'timeout_seconds': 20,\n        'max_results_per_day': 200,         # Hard limit\n        'respect_robots_txt': True,\n        'review_tos_required': True\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### Request Throttling Implementation\n\n```python\nfrom asyncio import sleep\nfrom time import time\n\nclass RateLimiter:\n    def __init__(self, requests_per_second: float):\n        self.min_interval = 1.0 / requests_per_second\n        self.last_request_time = 0\n\n    async def wait(self):\n        \"\"\"Wait until safe to make next request\"\"\"\n        elapsed = time() - self.last_request_time\n        if elapsed < self.min_interval:\n            await sleep(self.min_interval - elapsed)\n        self.last_request_time = time()\n```\n\n---\n\n## MONITORING & LOGGING\n\n### Crawler Health Metrics\n\n```python\nclass CrawlerMetrics:\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.total_urls_crawled = 0\n        self.successful_extractions = 0\n        self.failed_extractions = 0\n        self.timeout_errors = 0\n        self.rate_limit_errors = 0\n        self.total_documents_extracted = 0\n        self.last_crawl_timestamp = None\n\n    def get_health_status(self) -> Dict:\n        success_rate = (self.successful_extractions /\n                       (self.successful_extractions + self.failed_extractions))\n        return {\n            'success_rate': success_rate,\n            'urls_crawled': self.total_urls_crawled,\n            'documents_extracted': self.total_documents_extracted,\n            'timeout_rate': self.timeout_errors / self.total_urls_crawled,\n            'last_crawl': self.last_crawl_timestamp\n        }\n```\n\n### Logging Strategy\n\n```python\n# Standard format for all log entries\nLOG_FORMAT = {\n    'timestamp': 'ISO8601',\n    'source': 'source_name',\n    'url': 'full_url_crawled',\n    'status_code': 'HTTP status',\n    'extracted_items': 'count',\n    'duration_seconds': 'float',\n    'error': 'error_message if any',\n    'retry_attempt': 'int'\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## TESTING STRATEGY\n\n### Unit NOTES\n\n### What Works Well\n✓ Direct PDF access from NA and Senate\n✓ Consistent bill number format across sources\n✓ HTML table-based listings (easy to parse)\n✓ Multiple query parameters for filtering\n✓ No apparent login requirements for bills\n✓ Large archive of historical bills\n\n### Potential Issues\n⚠ Intermittent timeout issues (server load or geo-blocking)\n⚠ Provincial sites use VALIDATION CHECKLIST\n\nWhen you extract a bill, verify:\n- [ ] Bill number exists and is formatted correctly (e.g., \"91 of 2025\")\n- [ ] Title is non-empty and reasonable length (>5 chars)\n- [ ] Date is valid and within parliament session\n- [ ] Type is one of: Government, Private Member, Constitutional Amendment\n- [ ] Status is valid (Introduced, Passed, Pending, etc.)\n- [ ] Source URL is |\n|-------|-------------|----------|\n| Timeout errors | Server overload or geo-blocking | Increase timeout, add retry logic, use proxy if needed |\n| 429 Too Many Requests | Rate limiting | Increase delay between requests to 3-5 seconds |\n| Empty results | JavaScript-rendered content | Use Selenium/Playwright for browser automation |\n| PDF extraction fails | Scanned PDFs or poor quality | Implement OCR (tesseract) as fallback |\n| Duplicate bills | Multiple sources list same bill | Implement bill deduplication by number + title |\n| Missing fields | Page structure changed | Monitor Consistent bill numbering across sources\n✓ Multiple entry points for each source\n✓ Large historical archive available\n✓ No authentication required for bill data\n✓ Structured HTML listings\n\n### Challenges\n⚠ Intermittent timeout issues observed\n⚠ Some sites may be partially JavaScript-rendered\n⚠ Provincial sites have varied parameter structures\n⚠ PDF quality varies (some need OCR)\n⚠ No official APIs (must use HTML parsing)\n⚠ District courts database is very large (8M+ cases)\n\n### Mitigations\n1. Implement exponential backoff for timeouts\n2. Use Playwright/Selenium if JavaScript needed\n3. Build flexible parameter parser\n4. Integrate pytesseract for OCR\n5. Accept HTML parsing as standard approach\n6. Rate-limit district courts crawling strictly\n\n---\n\n## RECOMMENDED IMPLEMENTATION SEQUENCE\n\n### Week 1-2: MVP (National Assembly)\n- Setup project structure\n- Implement NA crawler\n- Build PDF   │ ◄──── 'NA', 'Senate', 'PA', etc.\n│ bill_number (varchar) UNIQUE    │ ◄──── '91 of 2025'\n│ title (text)                    │ ◄──── Bill title\n│ date_introduced (date)          │ ◄──── When introduced\n│ bill_type (enum)                │ ◄──── Government/Private/Amendment\n│ status (varchar)                │ ◄──── Passed/Pending/Referred\n│ mover (varchar)                 │ ◄──── Sponsor name\n│ full_text (text)                │ ◄──── Extracted from PDF\n│ source_url (text)               │ ◄──── Original source\n│ document_url (text)             │ ◄──── PDF/HTML link\n│ crawled_at (timestamp)          │ ◄──── When we crawled\n│ updated_at (timestamp)          │ ◄──── Last update\n│ data_quality_score (float)      │ ◄──── 0.0-1.0\n└─────────────────────────────────┘\n\nINDEXES:\n- source + bill_number (unique)\n- source + date_introduced\n- status\n- crawled_at\n```\n\n## Technology Stack\n\n### Core Components\n```\nWeb Framework: FastAPI          (for API)\nCrawler: requests + bs4         (HTTP + parsing)\nPDF: pdfplumber + pytesseract   (extraction + OCR)\nDB: PostgreSQL + SQLAlchemy     (storage)\nTask Queue: Celery + Redis      (scheduling)\nTesting: pytest                 (validation)\n```\n\n### Deployment\n```\nContainerization: Docker\nOrchestration: Docker Compose (dev) / Kubernetes (prod)\nMonitoring: Prometheus + Grafana\nLogging: ELK Stack\nCI/CD: GitHub Actions\n```\n\n## Crawler Configuration Examples\n\n### Conservative (Safe)\n```yaml\nrate_limit_seconds: 3\ntimeout: 15\nretries: 5\nbackoff_factor: 2\nconcurrent_connections: 1\n```\n\n### Balanced (Recommended)\n```yaml\nrate_limit_seconds: 2\ntimeout: 10\nretries: 3\nbackoff_factor: 2\nconcurrent_connections: 1\n```\n\n### Aggressive (Only for private servers)\n```yaml\nrate_limit_seconds: 1\ntimeout: 8\nretries: 2\nbackoff_factor: 2\nconcurrent_connections: 2\n```\n\n## Quality Assurance Checklist\n\n```\nDATA EXTRACTION\n├── ✓ Bill numbers match source format\n├── ✓ Titles are non-empty (>5 chars)\n├── ✓ Dates are valid and within parliament session\n├── ✓ Types are valid enum values\n├── ✓ Status matches known states\n├── ✓ URLs are accessible\n└── ✓ PDFs download successfully\n\nTEXT QUALITY\n├── ✓ Full text > 500 characters\n├── ✓ No excessive special characters\n├── ✓ Common words present (bill, act, section, etc.)\n├── ✓ Sentence structure intact\n└── ✓ OCR confidence > 85% (if OCR'd)\n\nDEDUPLICATION\n├── ✓ No duplicate bill_numbers per source\n├── ✓ Cross-source duplicates identified\n├── ✓ Merge candidates reviewed manually\n└── ✓ Source attribution preserved\n\nCOVERAGE\n├── ✓ All expected sources present\n├── ✓ All sessions represented\n├── ✓ No large gaps in years\n├── ✓ Historical archives complete\n└── ✓ Recent bills within 48 hours\n```\n\n## Monitoring Architecture\n\n```\n┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│                   CRAWLER ORCHESTRATOR                     │\n└────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n                           │\n     ┌─────────────────────┼─────────────────────┐\n     │                     │                     │\n┌────▼───┐           ┌─────▼─────┐         ┌───▼────┐\n│  URL   │           │  FETCHER  │         │ RATE   │\n│QUEUE   │──────────▶│ (requests)│────────▶│LIMITER │\n└────────┘           └─────┬─────┘         └────────┘\n                           │\n                      ┌────▼────┐\n                      │ PARSER  │\n                      │(BS4/    │\n                      │Selenium)│\n                      └────┬────┘\n                           │\n      ┌────────────────────┼────────────────────┐\n      │                    │                    │\n┌─────▼─────┐    ┌────────▼────────┐    ┌─────▼─────┐\n│HTML        │    │PDF EXTRACTOR   │    │DATA       │\n│EXTRACTOR   │    │(pdfplumber/    │    │NORMALIZER │\n│            │    │pytesseract)    │    │           │\n└─────┬─────┘    └────────┬────────┘    └─────┬─────┘\n      │                   │                    │\n      └───────────────────┼────────────────────┘\n                          │\n                    ┌─────▼──────┐\n                    │VALIDATION  │\n                    │(dedup,     │\n                    │quality     │\n                    │check)      │\n                    └─────┬──────┘\n                          │\n                    ┌─────▼──────┐\n                    │ DATABASE   │\n                    │(PostgreSQL)│\n                    └────────────┘\n```\n\n## Database Schema (Simplified)\n\n```\nTABLE: bills\n┌─────────────────────────────────┐\n│ id (UUID)                       │ ◄──── Primary Key\n│ source (varchar)                │ ◄──── 'NA', 'Senate', 'PA', etc.\n│ bill_number (varchar) UNIQUE    │ ◄──── '91 of 2025'\n│ title (text)                    │ ◄──── Bill title\n│ date_introduced (date)          │ ◄──── When introduced\n│ bill_type (enum)                │ ◄──── Government/Private/Amendment\n│ status (varchar)                │ ◄──── Passed/Pending/Referred\n│ mover (varchar)                 │ ◄──── Sponsor name\n│ full_text (text)                │ ◄──── Extracted from PDF\n│ source_url (text)               │ ◄──── Original source\n│ document_url (text)             │ ◄──── PDF/HTML link\n│ crawled_at (timestamp)          │ ◄──── When we crawled\n│ updated_at (timestamp)          │ ◄──── Last update\n│ data_quality_score (float)      │ ◄──── 0.0-1.0\n└─────────────────────────────────┘\n\nINDEXES:\n- source + bill_number (unique)\n- source + date_introduced\n- status\n- crawled_at\n```\n\n## Technology Stack\n\n### Core Components\n```\nWeb Framework: FastAPI          (for API)\nCrawler: requests + bs4         (HTTP + parsing)\nPDF: pdfplumber + pytesseract   (extraction + OCR)\nDB: PostgreSQL + SQLAlchemy     (storage)\nTask Queue: Celery + Redis      (scheduling)\nTesting: pytest                 (validation)\n```\n\n### Deployment\n```\nContainerization: Docker\nOrchestration: Docker Compose (dev) / Kubernetes (prod)\nMonitoring: Prometheus + Grafana\nLogging: ELK Stack\nCI/CD: GitHub Actions\n```\n\n## Crawler Configuration Examples\n\n### Conservative (Safe)\n```yaml\nrate_limit_seconds: 3\ntimeout: 15\nretries: 5\nbackoff_factor: 2\nconcurrent_connections: 1\n```\n\n### Balanced (Recommended)\n```yaml\nrate_limit_seconds: 2\ntimeout: 10\nretries: 3\nbackoff_factor: 2\nconcurrent_connections: 1\n```\n\n### Aggressive (Only for private servers)\n```yaml\nrate_limit_seconds: 1\ntimeout: 8\nretries: 2\nbackoff_factor: 2\nconcurrent_connections: 2\n```\n\n## Quality Assurance Checklist\n\n```\nDATA EXTRACTION\n├── ✓ Bill numbers match source format\n├── ✓ Titles are non-empty (>5 chars)\n├── ✓ Dates are valid and within parliament session\n├── ✓ Types are valid enum values\n├── ✓ Status matches known states\n├── ✓ URLs are accessible\n└── ✓ PDFs download successfully\n\nTEXT QUALITY\n├── ✓ Full text > 500 characters\n├── ✓ No excessive special characters\n├── ✓ Common words present (bill, act, section, etc.)\n├── ✓ Sentence structure intact\n└── ✓ OCR confidence > 85% (if OCR'd)\n\nDEDUPLICATION\n├── ✓ No duplicate bill_numbers per source\n├── ✓ Cross-source duplicates identified\n├── ✓ Merge candidates reviewed manually\n└── ✓ Source attribution preserved\n\nCOVERAGE\n├── ✓ All expected sources present\n├── ✓ All sessions represented\n├── ✓ No large gaps in years\n├── ✓ Historical archives complete\n└── ✓ Recent bills within 48 hours\n```\n\n## Monitoring Dashboard\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│           CRAWLER HEALTH DASHBOARD Legal analysis?\n   - Legislative tracking?\n   - Research database?\n   - This affects data model and features\n\n### Starting Code\n\n1. **Setup Project** (2-3 hours)\n   - Create Python project structure\n   - HTTP requests\nbeautifulsoup4    - HTML parsing\nselenium/playwright - JavaScript rendering (if needed)\n```\n\n### PDF Processing\n```\npdfplumber        - PDF text extraction\npytesseract       - OCR for scanned PDFs\n```\n\n### Data Storage\n```\nPostgreSQL        - Relational database\nSQLAlchemy        - ORM\n```\n\n### Task Scheduling\n```\nCelery            - Distributed task queue\nRedis             - Message broker and cache\n```\n\n### API\n```\nFastAPI           - Web framework\npydantic          - Data validation\n```\n\n### Testing\n```\npytest            - Unit testing\npytest-asyncio    - Async testing\n```\n\n### Deployment\n```\nDocker            - Containerization\ndocker-compose    - Local orchestration\nKubernetes        - Production orchestration (optional)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Expected Challenges & Solutions\n\n| Challenge | Solution |\n|-----------|----------|\n| Intermittent timeouts | Implement exponential backoff, increase timeout to 15s |\n| JavaScript-rendered content | Use Selenium/Playwright for browser automation |\n| PDF extraction quality | Use OCR fallback (pytesseract) for low confidence |\n| Large volume (8M+ district court cases) | Implement strict rate limiting (5+ sec delay) |\n| Site structure changes | Automated tests with CI/CD pipeline |\n| Duplicate bills across sources | Implement bill deduplication by number + title |\n| Rate limiting | Conservative 2-3 second delays, monitor for 429 errors |\n\n---\n\n## Success Indicators\n\n### Week 2 (MVP)\n- ✓ National Assembly crawler operational\n- ✓ 850 bills extracted and stored\n- ✓ 98%+ extraction accuracy\n- ✓ Tests passing\n\n### Week 4 (Expansion)\n- ✓ All federal + provincial crawlers working\n- ✓ 2,500+ bills in database\n- ✓ Deduplication complete\n- ✓ API endpoint functional\n\n### Week 6 (Production)\n- ✓ Scheduled crawling operational\n- ✓ Change detection working\n- ✓ Monitoring & alerting active\n- ✓ 99.5%+ uptime\n\n---\n\n## File Locations\n\nAll documents are located in: `/Users/umerkhan/code/`\n\n```\n/Users/umerkhan/code/\n├── VERIFICATION-SUMMARY.md                          (Executive summary)\n├── pakistani-legislative-sources-verification.md    (Complete report)\n├── pakistan-crawler-technical-specs.md              (Implementation guide)\n├── pakistan-sources-quick-reference.md              (Quick reference)\n├── IMPLEMENTATION-ROADMAP.md                        (Project plan)\n└── README-PAKISTAN-CRAWLER.md                       (This file)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Questions to Answer Before Implementation\n\n1. **What's the primary use case?**\n   - Legal analysis, research, legislative tracking, public portal?\n   - This affects data model and features\n\n2. **What's the update frequency needed?**\n   - Real-time? Daily? Weekly? Monthly?\n   - Affects crawling schedule\n\n3. **Will you need Urdu text?**\n   - Some sources have Urdu versions\n   - Requires additional parsing\n\n4. **How to handle related documents?**\n   - Committee reports, amendments, clauses?\n   - Affects data model\n\n5. **Storage backend?**\n   - PostgreSQL recommended for structured data\n   - MongoDB if more flexible schema needed\n\n6. **Need API for public access?**\n   - FastAPI recommended for REST API\n   - Affects deployment strategy\n\n7. **How often to re-crawl existing bills?**\n   - For status updates on pending bills\n   - Affects scheduling logic\n\n---\n\n## Contact & Support\n\nIf you encounter issues during implementation:\n\n1. **robots.txt blocked?** - Try identifying yourself with User-Agent header\n2. **Rate limited (429)?** - Increase delay between requests (3-5 seconds)\n3. **Timeouts (408/504)?** - Increase timeout value (15-20 seconds)\n4. **PDF extraction fails?** - Check PDF quality, use OCR as fallback\n5. **Site structure changed?** - Update CSS selectors, implement automated testing\n\n---\n\n## Legal Notice\n\nAll sources verified are public government websites. Legislative documents are typically public domain. However:\n\n- **Always verify robots.txt** before crawling\n- **Review Terms of Service** on each site\n- **Check local laws** regarding data scraping in your jurisdiction\n- **Provide attribution** to source in your data\n- **Respect rate limiting** to avoid overloading servers\n\n---\n\n## Version History\n\n| Version | Date | Status | Changes |\n|---------|------|--------|---------|\n| 1.0 |
